      <h1 id="user-content-css-z-index-007" class="deep-link package-name-redundant"><a href="#css-z-index-007">css-z-index 0.0.7</a></h1>
<p class="package-description-redundant">Css module of single purpose classes for z index</p>

<h2 id="user-content-installation" class="deep-link"><a href="#installation">Installation</a></h2>
<h4>With <a href="https://npmjs.com">npm</a></h4>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>npm&#xA0;install&#xA0;--save-dev&#xA0;css-z-index</span></span></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="user-content-with-git" class="deep-link"><a href="#with-git">With Git</a></h4>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>git&#xA0;clone&#xA0;</span><span class="markup underline link hyperlink"><span>https://github.com/tachyons-css/css-z-index</span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="user-content-usage" class="deep-link"><a href="#usage">Usage</a></h2>
<h4>Using with <a href="https://github.com/postcss/postcss">PostCSS</a></h4>
<p>Import the css module</p>
<div class="highlight css"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta at-rule import css"><span class="keyword control at-rule import css"><span class="punctuation definition keyword css"><span>@</span></span><span>import</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="string quoted double css"><span class="punctuation definition string begin css"><span>&quot;</span></span><span>css-z-index</span><span class="punctuation definition string end css"><span>&quot;</span></span></span></span><span>;</span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>Then process the CSS using the <a href="https://github.com/tachyons-css/tachyons-cli"><code>tachyons-cli</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight sh"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source shell"><span>$&#xA0;npm&#xA0;i&#xA0;-g&#xA0;tachyons-cli</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source shell"><span>$&#xA0;tachyons-cli&#xA0;path/to/css-file.css&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator shell"><span>&gt;</span></span><span>&#xA0;dist/t.css</span></span></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="user-content-using-the-css" class="deep-link"><a href="#using-the-css">Using the CSS</a></h4>
<p>The built CSS is located in the <code>css</code> directory. It contains an unminified and minified version.
You can either cut and paste that css or link to it directly in your html.</p>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text html"><span class="meta tag inline any html"><span class="punctuation definition tag begin html"><span>&lt;</span></span><span class="entity name tag inline any html"><span>link</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="entity other attribute-name html"><span>rel</span></span><span>=</span><span class="string quoted double html"><span class="punctuation definition string begin html"><span>&quot;</span></span><span>stylesheet</span><span class="punctuation definition string end html"><span>&quot;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="entity other attribute-name html"><span>href</span></span><span>=</span><span class="string quoted double html"><span class="punctuation definition string begin html"><span>&quot;</span></span><span>path/to/module/css/css-z-index</span><span class="punctuation definition string end html"><span>&quot;</span></span></span><span class="punctuation definition tag end html"><span>&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="user-content-development" class="deep-link"><a href="#development">Development</a></h4>
<p>The source CSS files can be found in the <code>src</code> directory.
Running <code>$ npm start</code> will process the source CSS and place the built CSS in the <code>css</code> directory.</p>

    <a href="/package/z-i18n">z-i18n</a>
      <i class="icon-public"></i>
  </h1>
  <p class="package-description">Translation module with dynamic json storage in Redis and suport npm: express, z-form...</p>

  <form class="star">

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 id="user-content-multi-language-z-i18n-with-redis-io" class="deep-link package-name-redundant"><a href="#multi-language-z-i18n-with-redis-io">Multi language z-i18n with Redis IO</a></h1>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Download and install test project at (New version 1.0.2): <a href="https://github.com/kimthangatm/test-node-js-z-i18n/">https://github.com/kimthangatm/test-node-js-z-i18n/</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>New tutorial Node Js Mutiple language &amp; more .. at : <a href="https://kimtatthang.wordpress.com/2015/03/11/multiple-languages-i18n-l10n-in-your-node-js-express-and-redis/">https://kimtatthang.wordpress.com/2015/03/11/multiple-languages-i18n-l10n-in-your-node-js-express-and-redis/</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Translation module with dynamic json storage in Redis and suport npm: express, z-form...</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>When APP Node JS firt run, translation loaded loaded from file or Redis and never reload =&gt; Fast</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 id="user-content-example-integrate-z-i18n-with-express--redis" class="deep-link"><a href="#example-integrate-z-i18n-with-express--redis">Example integrate z-i18n with Express + Redis</a></h1>
<h2 id="user-content-step-1-install-redis" class="deep-link"><a href="#step-1-install-redis">Step 1: Install Redis</a></h2>
<p>My computer is MacOS 10.10.2 and currently Redis version is 2.8.19, you can use guide bellow or visit: <a href="http://redis.io/download">http://redis.io/download</a> to download and install redis server</p>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>//Mac&#xA0;OS&#xA0;install</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;wget&#xA0;</span><span class="markup underline link hyperlink"><span>http://download.redis.io/releases/redis-2.8.19.tar.gz</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;tar&#xA0;xzf&#xA0;redis-2.8.19.tar.gz</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;cd&#xA0;redis-2.8.19</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;make</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;sudo&#xA0;make&#xA0;install</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>//&#xA0;Restart&#xA0;redis&#xA0;in&#xA0;background&#xA0;Mac&#xA0;OS</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;redis-server&#xA0;&gt;&#xA0;/dev/null&#xA0;&amp;</span></span></div></pre></div>
<p><strong>Note:</strong> <code>When Node Js application running, translation save on Redis, if you want reload cache please follow:</code></p>
<p><em>Typing into terminal</em></p>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;redis-cli</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>//Result:&#xA0;127.0.0.1:6379&gt;</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;FLUSHALL</span></span></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="user-content-step-2-create-new-project-with-express-generator" class="deep-link"><a href="#step-2-create-new-project-with-express-generator">Step 2: Create new project with Express Generator</a></h2>
<p><code>Open terminal and typing</code></p>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>//&#xA0;#&#xA0;If&#xA0;you&#xA0;don&apos;t&#xA0;have&#xA0;express&#xA0;generator:</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>//&#xA0;#&#xA0;sudo&#xA0;npm&#xA0;install&#xA0;express-generator&#xA0;-g</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>cd&#xA0;~</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>express&#xA0;test-i18n&#xA0;&amp;amp;&amp;amp;&#xA0;cd&#xA0;test-i18n</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>sudo&#xA0;npm&#xA0;install</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>sudo&#xA0;npm&#xA0;install&#xA0;redis&#xA0;z-i18n</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>sudo&#xA0;npm&#xA0;update</span></span></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="user-content-step-3-create-translation-file" class="deep-link"><a href="#step-3-create-translation-file">Step 3: Create translation file</a></h2>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>test-i18n/</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>&#x2514;&#x2500;&#x2500;&#xA0;languages</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#x251C;&#x2500;&#x2500;&#xA0;en_GB</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#x2502;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#x2514;&#x2500;&#x2500;&#xA0;moduleA.en_GB.json</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#x2514;&#x2500;&#x2500;&#xA0;nl_NL</span></span></div><div class="line"><span <p><code>Open terminal and typing</code></p>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>//cd&#xA0;&quot;path_project&quot;</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>cd&#xA0;~/test-i18n/</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>node&#xA0;bin/www</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>//&#xA0;If&#xA0;you&#xA0;have&#xA0;grunt</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>grunt</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>//&#xA0;If&#xA0;you&#xA0;have&#xA0;nodemon</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>nodemon</span></span></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="user-content-step-8-testing-on-browser" class="deep-link"><a href="#step-8-testing-on-browser">Step 8: Testing on browser:</a></h2>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Address: <code>127.0.0.1:3000</code> . App use default <code>&#x201C;en_GB&#x201D;</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Address: <code>127.0.0.1:3000?lang=nl_NL</code> . App switch <code>language &#x201C;nl_NL&#x201D;</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Address: <code>127.0.0.1:3000?lang=vi_VN</code> . Because <code>&#x201C;vi_VN&#x201D;</code> lang don&#x2019;t have tranlation key &#x201C;hello_user_name&#x201D;, system get default <code>&#x201C;hello_user_name&#x201D;</code> in <code>default_language = &#x201C;en_GB&#x201D;</code></p>
</li>
</ol>

json"><span>9999</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source json"><span class="meta structure dictionary json"><span class="meta structure dictionary json"><span class="meta structure array json"><span class="meta structure dictionary json"><span class="meta structure dictionary json"><span>&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;</span></span><span class="punctuation definition dictionary end json"><span>}</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source json"><span class="meta structure dictionary json"><span class="meta structure dictionary json"><span class="meta structure array <h2 id="user-content-details" class="deep-link"><a href="#details">Details</a></h2>
<div class="highlight css"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity name tag css"><span>a</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>10</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="comment block css"><span class="punctuation definition comment css"><span>/*</span></span><span>*&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#x2191;</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="comment block css"><span>&#xA0;*&#xA0;This&#xA0;number&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation definition comment css"><span>*/</span></span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>From <a href="https://css-tricks.com/handling-z-index/">CSS Tricks article</a>:</p>
<blockquote>
<p>It&apos;s fairly common to see people number in the hundreds with z-index in web design too. The idea being that you could slip something in between later if need be, which you couldn&apos;t if you did 1, 2, 3, etc, because z-index doesn&apos;t support decimals.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>This rule also handles negative values.</p>
<h3 id="user-content-options" class="deep-link"><a href="#options">Options</a></h3>
<h4 id="user-content--min-10-" class="deep-link"><a href="#-min-10-"><code>{ min: 10 }</code></a></h4>
<p>The following patterns are considered warnings:</p>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 id="user-content-grunt-z-schema" class="deep-link package-name-redundant"><a href="#grunt-z-schema">grunt-z-schema</a></h1>
<p class="package-description-redundant">Grunt plugin for <a href="https://github.com/zaggino/z-schema">z-schema</a>, a JSON Schema validator.</p>
<h2 id="user-content-getting-started" class="deep-link"><a href="#getting-started">Getting Started</a></h2>
<p>This plugin requires Grunt.</p>
<p>If you haven&apos;t used <a href="http://gruntjs.com/">Grunt</a> before, be sure to check out the <a href="http://gruntjs.com/getting-started">Getting Started</a> guide, as it explains how to create a <a href="http://gruntjs.com/sample-gruntfile">Gruntfile</a> as well as install and use Grunt plugins. Once you&apos;re familiar with that process, you may install this plugin with this command:</p>
<div class="highlight shell"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source shell"><span>npm&#xA0;install&#xA0;grunt-z-schema&#xA0;--save-dev</span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>Once the plugin has been installed, it may be enabled inside your Gruntfile with this line of JavaScript:</p>
<div class="highlight js"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span class="variable other object js"><span>grunt</span></span><span class="meta js"><span class="meta delimiter method period js"><span>.</span></span><span class="entity name function js"><span>loadNpmTasks</span></span><span class="meta js"><span class="punctuation definition begin round js"><span>(</span></span><span class="string quoted single js"><span class="punctuation definition string begin js"><span>&apos;</span></span><span>grunt-z-schema</span><span class="punctuation definition string end js"><span>&apos;</span></span></span><span class="punctuation definition end round js"><span>)</span></span></span></span><span class="punctuation terminator statement js"><span>;</span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="user-content-the-zschema-task" class="deep-link"><a href="#the-zschema-task">The &quot;zschema&quot; task</a></h2>
<h3 id="user-content-overview" class="deep-link"><a href="#overview">Overview</a></h3>
<p>In your project&apos;s Gruntfile, add a section named <code>zschema</code> to the data object passed into <code>grunt.initConfig()</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight js"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span class="variable other object js"><span>grunt</span></span><span class="meta js"><span <h3 id="user-content-options" class="deep-link"><a href="#options">Options</a></h3>
<p>Options for <a href="https://github.com/zaggino/z-schema#strict-validation">strict validation</a>. Any option defined here will be passed over to ZSchema instance.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="highlight js"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>zschema</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta brace curly js"><span>{</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>&#xA0;&#xA0;options</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta brace curly js"><span>{</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;&#xA0;noTypeless</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant language boolean true js"><span>true</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>&#xA0;&#xA0;</span><span class="meta brace curly js"><span>}</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span class="meta brace curly js"><span>}</span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="user-content-usage-examples" class="deep-link"><a href="#usage-examples">Usage Examples</a></h3>
<p>In this example, <code>post1.json</code> and <code>post2.json</code> are two JSON files that will be validated against the <code>post-schema.json</code> schema. All JSON files in the <code>comments</code> will be validated against the comment schema. All validations will also report unknown keywords.</p>
<div class="highlight js"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span class="variable other object js"><span>grunt</span></span><span class="meta js"><span <h2 id="user-content-contributing" class="deep-link"><a href="#contributing">Contributing</a></h2>

<h3 id="user-content-tests" class="deep-link"><a href="#tests">Tests</a></h3>
<pre><code>npm test
</code></pre>
<p>The test will print out validation errors for the tasks designed to fail. That is expected behaviour. Unfortunately, Grunt does not really provide a good way to test that a task failed. If you come across a better solution please let me know.</p>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 id="user-content-tachyons-z-index-123" class="deep-link package-name-redundant"><a href="#tachyons-z-index-123">tachyons-z-index 1.2.3</a></h1>
<p>Base CSS module for Tachyons</p>
<h4 id="user-content-stats" class="deep-link"><a href="#stats">Stats</a></h4>

<h2 id="user-content-installation" class="deep-link"><a href="#installation">Installation</a></h2>
<h4>With <a href="https://npmjs.com">npm</a></h4>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>npm&#xA0;install&#xA0;--save-dev&#xA0;tachyons-z-index</span></span></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="user-content-with-git" class="deep-link"><a href="#with-git">With Git</a></h4>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>git&#xA0;clone&#xA0;</span><span class="markup underline link hyperlink"><span>https://github.com/tachyons-css/tachyons-z-index</span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="user-content-usage" class="deep-link"><a href="#usage">Usage</a></h2>
<h4>Using with <a href="https://github.com/postcss/postcss">PostCSS</a></h4>
<p>Import the css module</p>
<div class="highlight css"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta at-rule import css"><span class="keyword control at-rule import css"><span class="punctuation definition keyword css"><span>@</span></span><span>import</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="string quoted double css"><span class="punctuation definition string begin css"><span>&quot;</span></span><span>tachyons-z-index</span><span class="punctuation definition string end css"><span>&quot;</span></span></span></span><span>;</span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>Then process the CSS using the <a href="https://github.com/tachyons-css/tachyons-cli"><code>tachyons-cli</code></a></p>
<div class="highlight sh"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source shell"><span>$&#xA0;npm&#xA0;i&#xA0;-g&#xA0;tachyons-cli</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source shell"><span>$&#xA0;tachyons-cli&#xA0;path/to/css-file.css&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator shell"><span>&gt;</span></span><span>&#xA0;dist/t.css</span></span></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="user-content-using-the-css" class="deep-link"><a href="#using-the-css">Using the CSS</a></h4>
<p>The built CSS is located in the <code>css</code> directory. It contains an unminified and minified version.
You can either cut and paste that css or link to it directly in your html.</p>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text html"><span class="meta tag inline any html"><span class="punctuation definition tag begin html"><span>&lt;</span></span><span class="entity name tag inline any html"><span>link</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="entity other attribute-name html"><span>rel</span></span><span>=</span><span class="string quoted double html"><span class="punctuation definition string begin html"><span>&quot;</span></span><span>stylesheet</span><span class="punctuation definition string end html"><span>&quot;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="entity other attribute-name html"><span>href</span></span><span>=</span><span class="string quoted double html"><span class="punctuation definition string begin html"><span>&quot;</span></span><span>path/to/module/css/tachyons-z-index</span><span class="punctuation definition string end html"><span>&quot;</span></span></span><span class="punctuation definition tag end html"><span>&gt;</span></span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="user-content-development" class="deep-link"><a href="#development">Development</a></h4>
<p>The source CSS files can be found in the <code>src</code> directory.
Running <code>$ npm start</code> will process the source CSS and place the built CSS in the <code>css</code> directory.</p>

  <h1 class="package-name">
    <a href="/package/z-index">z-index</a>
      <i class="icon-public"></i>
  </h1>
  <p class="package-description">Dead simple CSS z-index utilities.</p>

  <form class="star">
    <input type="hidden" name="name" value="z-index">
    <input id="star-input" type="checkbox" name="isStarred" value="true" >
    <label for="star-input" class="icon-star"></label>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 id="user-content-z-index" class="deep-link package-name-redundant"><a href="#z-index">z-index</a></h1>
<p class="package-description-redundant">A tiny and dead simple set of CSS z-index utilities.</p>
<h2 id="user-content-why" class="deep-link"><a href="#why">why</a></h2>
<p>The z space in CSS can easily become arbitrarily increased over time as new
components are added. You&apos;ve probably seen something like this before in CSS
source code...</p>
<div class="highlight css"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="comment block css"><span class="punctuation definition comment css"><span>/*</span></span><span>&#xA0;need&#xA0;this&#xA0;to&#xA0;go&#xA0;above&#xA0;the&#xA0;other&#xA0;thing&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation definition comment css"><span>*/</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>og-component</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>9</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>and some time later...</p>
<div class="highlight css"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="comment block css"><span class="punctuation definition comment css"><span>/*</span></span><span>&#xA0;this&#xA0;needs&#xA0;to&#xA0;go&#xA0;above&#xA0;og-component&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation definition comment css"><span>*/</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>new-component</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>10</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>newer-component</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>11</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>In practice we generally don&apos;t need more than a few layers at any one time
even across fairly complex apps.</p>
<p>By adopting a small range of values that mimics the (inverse) of the HTML heading
spec, that we can apply directly to any html element, we prevent the need to
declare z-indexes on the fly, and keep the mental model of &quot;layers&quot; easy to
understand while developing.</p>
<div class="highlight css"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>z1</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>1</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>z2</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>2</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>z3</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>3</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>z4</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>4</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>z5</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>5</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>z6</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>6</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>Other than the 6 basic indexes, a <code>zF</code> class is included that forces a very high
z-index in the event that another component or library is being overzealous
with its z-index values and you just can&apos;t even.</p>
<div class="highlight css"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>zF</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>999</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="comment block css"><span class="punctuation definition comment css"><span>/*</span></span><span>&#xA0;break&#xA0;glass&#xA0;in&#xA0;case&#xA0;of&#xA0;emergency&#xA0;</span><span class="punctuation definition comment css"><span>*/</span></span></span></span></div></pre></div>

      <h1 id="user-content-sass-z-indexer" class="deep-link package-name-redundant"><a href="#sass-z-indexer">sass-z-indexer</a></h1>
<p class="package-description-redundant">A handy Sass helper for managing z-index layers</p>
<h2 id="user-content-install" class="deep-link"><a href="#install">Install</a></h2>
<pre><code>$ npm install --save sass-z-indexer
$ bower install --save sass-z-indexer
</code></pre>
<h2 id="user-content-use" class="deep-link"><a href="#use">Use</a></h2>
<pre><code>my-element{
 z-index: z(&quot;overlay&quot;);
}
</code></pre>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 class="package-name-redundant">postcss-z <a href="https://travis-ci.org/AgtLucas/postcss-z"><img src="https://travis-ci.org/AgtLucas/postcss-z.svg?branch=master" class="badge"></a></h1>
<p class="package-description-redundant">A PostCSS plugin to replace z with z-index.</p>
<h2 id="user-content-example" class="deep-link"><a href="#example">Example</a></h2>
<p>Input:</p>
<div class="highlight css"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>blackbriar</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta css"><span>&#xA0;&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span>z</span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>1</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div></pre></div>

<div class="highlight css"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta selector css"><span class="entity other attribute-name class css"><span class="punctuation definition entity css"><span>.</span></span><span>blackbriar</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span></span><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section begin css"><span>{</span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta css"><span>&#xA0;&#xA0;</span><span class="meta property-name css"><span class="support type property-name css"><span>z-index</span></span></span><span class="meta property-value css"><span class="punctuation separator key-value css"><span>:</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="constant numeric css"><span>1</span></span><span class="punctuation terminator rule css"><span>;</span></span></span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source css"><span class="meta css"><span class="punctuation section end css"><span>}</span></span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="user-content-usage" class="deep-link"><a href="#usage">Usage</a></h2>
<p>Install:</p>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>npm&#xA0;i&#xA0;-D&#xA0;postcss-z</span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>Then include the plugin:</p>
<div class="highlight js"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span class="meta function-call js"><span class="entity name function js"><span>postcss</span></span><span class="meta js"><span class="punctuation definition begin round js"><span>(</span></span><span class="meta brace square js"><span>[</span></span><span class="meta function-call js"><span class="support function js"><span>require</span></span><span class="meta js"><span class="punctuation definition begin round js"><span>(</span></span><span class="string quoted single js"><span class="punctuation definition string begin js"><span>&apos;</span></span><span>postcss-z</span><span class="punctuation definition string end js"><span>&apos;</span></span></span><span class="punctuation definition end round js"><span>)</span></span></span></span><span class="meta brace round js"><span>(</span></span><span>options</span><span class="meta brace round js"><span>)</span></span><span class="meta brace square js"><span>]</span></span><span class="punctuation definition end round js"><span>)</span></span></span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>See <a href="https://github.com/postcss/postcss">PostCSS</a> docs for examples for your environment.</p>

<div class="content-column">

  <h1 class="package-name">
    <a href="/package/z-math">z-math</a>
      <i class="icon-public"></i>
  </h1>
  <p class="package-description">A simple module for operations on arbitrarily large integers, because sometimes 64-bit floats don&#x27;t quite cut it.</p>

  <form class="star">
    <input type="hidden" name="name" value="z-math">
    <input id="star-input" type="checkbox" name="isStarred" value="true" >
    <label for="star-input" class="icon-star"></label>
      <input type="hidden" name="crumb" value="6iU2ZDDsuwGmTByLveTURCTRcXf7f6w7tDg9-heJAHf"/>
  </form>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 id="user-content-z-math" class="deep-link package-name-redundant"><a href="#z-math">z-math</a></h1>
<p class="badge-only"><a href="https://travis-ci.org/joshuacaron/z-math"><img src="https://travis-ci.org/joshuacaron/z-math.svg?branch=master" class="badge"></a></p>
<p>A simple module for operations on arbitrarily large integers, because sometimes 64-bit floats don&apos;t quite cut it. In future versions, I plan to add support for operations on Z_n (i.e. modular arithmetic and multiplication), as well as some common number theory algorithms such as calculating gcd, lcm, etc.</p>
<h2 id="user-content-usage" class="deep-link"><a href="#usage">Usage</a></h2>
<p>To download the package simply run <code>npm install --save z-math</code>. Then just require it into your app like follows, and you are good to go: <code>var integer = require(&apos;z-math&apos;)</code></p>
<p>Once you have the package imported you can create new integers with the <code>integer(n)</code> command where n is a regular integer in Javascript (technically a floating point number).</p>
<p>To convert an integer, say <code>a</code>, back to a JavaScript float use <code>a.toFloat()</code> or use it in the context of a mathematical operation, e.g. <code>a + 5</code>.</p>
<p>To convert an integer, say <code>b</code>, to a string, use <code>b.toString()</code>, or use it in the context of a string e.g. <code>console.log(&apos;The integer is: &apos; + b)</code></p>
<h2 id="user-content-operations" class="deep-link"><a href="#operations">Operations</a></h2>
<p>Then the remaining operations are defined as follows:</p>
<p>Add 2 integers: <code>integer.add(a, b)</code></p>
<p>Subtract 2 integers: <code>integer.subtract(a, b)</code></p>
<p>Multiply 2 integers: <code>integer.multiply(a, b)</code></p>
<p>Get the quotient when dividing 2 integers: <code>integer.quotient(a, b)</code></p>
<p>Get the modulus when dividing 2 integers: <code>integer.mod(a, b)</code></p>
<p>Find a to the power of b: <code>integer.pow(a, b)</code></p>
<p>To test equality/inequality there are a number of functions: <code>integer.greaterThan</code>, <code>integer.lessThan</code>, <code>integer.equal</code>, <code>integer.notEqual</code>, <code>integer.greaterThanEqual</code>, <code>integer.lessThanEqual</code></p>
<p>Note that you can use <code>integer.lte</code> and <code>integer.gte</code> as shortcuts for <code>integer.lessThanEqual</code> and <code>integer.greaterThanEqual</code> respectively.</p>
<p><strong>All of these operations return new integers and leave the original ones untouched.</strong></p>

  </div>

</div>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1><img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/leonardiwagner/z/master/z-logo.png"> <a href="https://travis-ci.org/leonardiwagner/z"><img src="https://travis-ci.org/leonardiwagner/z.svg?branch=master" class="badge"></a></h1>
<p class="package-description-redundant">Native pattern matching for Javascript.</p>
<h3 id="user-content-usage" class="deep-link"><a href="#usage">Usage</a></h3>
<ul>
<li>install via npm: <code>npm install z</code></li>
<li>require <strong>z</strong> library in your code</li>
<li><strong>z</strong> implements <code>matches</code> function in Arrays, Strings and Numbers for pattern matching, example:</li>
</ul>

<p>The example above is using Javascript ECMAScript 6 (ES6), but you can use <strong>z</strong> with traditional JavaScript as well, just isn&apos;t that pretty:</p>

<p>The pattern matching &quot;trick&quot; in <strong>z</strong> is: each match is a function, where function parameters describes the pattern. Simple and powerful, eh?</p>
<h3 id="user-content-available-patterns" class="deep-link"><a href="#available-patterns">Available Patterns</a></h3>
<ul>
<li><code>() =&gt;</code> matches empty (array or string) eg.: <code>[]</code>, <code>&apos;&apos;</code></li>
<li><code>(x) =&gt;</code> matches an array with a single element eg.: <code>[1]</code>, <code>[[1, 2, 3]]</code> (array with a single array), matches single character eg.: <code>&apos;x&apos;</code> or matches a single number eg.:<code>1</code></li>
<li><code>(x, xs)</code> =&gt; matches array with more than one element. First parameter is the first element (head), second is others (tail)</li>
<li><code>(x, y, xs)</code> =&gt; matches array with more than two elements. First parameter is the first element (head), second parameter is the second element, third are others (tail). You can specify more than 2 items eg.: <code>(x, y, z, xs)</code>, <code>(a, b, c, d, e, f, g, tail)</code>, etc...</li>
</ul>
<p>Rule of thumb: when the match has more than one parameter, the last parameter will be always the end of the array (tail).</p>
<h3 id="user-content-patterns-with-value-comparison" class="deep-link"><a href="#patterns-with-value-comparison">Patterns with value comparison</a></h3>
<p>NOTE: This is only available on ES6 with default parameters.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>(x = &apos;some value&apos;)</code> matches if the element has the specified value. The value can be anything, such as array, number, string, null, undefined, etc...</li>
<li><code>(x, xs = [])</code> same match above but with tail. It can match any value as well.</li>
</ul>
<p>Value comparison in pattern matching is very powerful and makes the code cleaner, eg.:</p>
<div class="highlight javascript"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span class="storage type js"><span>var</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta <h3 id="user-content-this-is-amazing-why-nobody-did-this-before-on-javascript" class="deep-link"><a href="#this-is-amazing-why-nobody-did-this-before-on-javascript">This is amazing! Why nobody did this before on JavaScript?</a></h3>
<p><a href="https://github.com/natefaubion">He did</a>, years ago! But <a href="https://github.com/natefaubion/matches.js">his first and greater Javascript pattern match library</a> create matches with strings, and this is ugly! (sorry). Maybe he thought this is ugly too and <a href="https://github.com/natefaubion/sparkler">he did a new pattern matching library</a> without strings, but need to install some macro stuff.. and well, I don&apos;t think that&apos;s nice either.</p>
<p>Why <strong>z</strong> was created? Because <em>IT&apos;S BEAUTIFUL</em>: No need to install nothing but the actual <strong>z</strong> library, the matches are real native javascript code, the patterns are written naturally, pure &#x2764;&#xFE0F;. Of course it hasn&apos;t all the features on these mentioned libraries due JavaScript limitations, but it supports the most used patterns to work with arrays, enhancing recursion and immutability code writing.</p>

<h3 id="user-content-helper-methods" class="deep-link"><a href="#helper-methods">Helper methods</a></h3>
<p>Besides <code>matches</code>, <strong>z</strong> also provides 4 new methods in JavaScript Arrays to facilitate working with recursion and immutability</p>
<ul>
<li><code>head</code> eg.: <code>[1, 2, 3, 4].head()</code> returns <code>1</code></li>
<li><code>last</code> eg.: <code>[1, 2, 3, 4].last()</code> returns <code>4</code></li>
<li><code>init</code> eg.: <code>[1, 2, 3, 4].init()</code> returns <code>[1, 2, 3]</code></li>
<li><code>tail</code> eg.: <code>[1, 2, 3, 4].tail()</code> returns <code>[2, 3, 4]</code></li>
</ul>
<h3 id="user-content-the-project-is-new-and-growing" class="deep-link"><a href="#the-project-is-new-and-growing">The project is new and growing!</a></h3>
<p>I expect some help for new ideas, bug report, pull requests, and making new friends &#x1F46F;&#x1F46F;</p>
<p>Don&apos;t be afraid, I&apos;m not expert on functional programming, so I really need help, feel free to contact me &#x1F44D;</p>

    <a href="/package/z-combinator">z-combinator</a>
      <i class="icon-public"></i>
  </h1>
  <p class="package-description">Z Combinator for self-referencing anonymous functions</p>

  <form class="star">
    <input type="hidden" name="name" value="z-combinator">

    <label for="star-input" class="icon-star"></label>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 id="user-content-z-combinator" class="deep-link package-name-redundant"><a href="#z-combinator">Z Combinator</a></h1>
<img src="http://www.threadbombing.com/data/media/67/Recursive_shades.gif">
<p><strong>Version:</strong> <em>0.1.1</em><br>
<strong>Master build:</strong> <a href="https://travis-ci.org/adlawson/z-combinator"><img src="https://travis-ci.org/adlawson/z-combinator.png?branch=master" class="badge"></a><br>
<strong>Develop build:</strong> <a href="https://travis-ci.org/adlawson/z-combinator"><img src="https://travis-ci.org/adlawson/z-combinator.png?branch=develop" class="badge"></a><br></p>
<p>This library provides a utility function to support the creation of self-referencing anonymous functions.<br>
It can be installed in whichever way you prefer, but I recommend <a href="https://npmjs.org/package/z-combinator">NPM</a>.</p>
<p>The Z Combinator is the same, in principle, as the Y Combinator except it works in languages with applicative (eager)
order of execution (arguments are evaluated before the function call) just like JavaScript.</p>
<p>For more information about the Z Combinator please read Douglas Crockford&apos;s <a href="http://www.crockford.com/javascript/little.html">&quot;The Little JavaScripter&quot;</a>.</p>
<h3 id="user-content-basic-usage" class="deep-link"><a href="#basic-usage">Basic usage</a></h3>

<h3 id="user-content-beware-of-infinite-recursion" class="deep-link"><a href="#beware-of-infinite-recursion">Beware of infinite recursion!</a></h3>
<p>Just as you would with any other recursive function, make sure you include some sort of break condition.
If you miss it out, the function will recur indefinitely.</p>
<div class="highlight js"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span class="storage type js"><span>var</span></span><span>&#xA0;z&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator assignment js"><span>=</span></span><span>&#xA0;</span><span class="meta function-call js"><span class="support function js"><span>require</span></span><span class="meta <h3 id="user-content-contributing" class="deep-link"><a href="#contributing">Contributing</a></h3>
<p>I accept contributions to the source via Pull Request,
but passing unit tests must be included before it will be considered for merge.</p>
<div class="highlight bash"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;make&#xA0;install</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;make&#xA0;tests</span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>If you have <a href="http://vagrantup.com">Vagrant</a> installed, you can build the dev environment to assist development.
The repository will be mounted in <code>/srv</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight bash"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;vagrant&#xA0;up</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;vagrant&#xA0;ssh</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>&#xA0;</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>Welcome&#xA0;to&#xA0;Ubuntu&#xA0;12.04&#xA0;LTS&#xA0;(GNU/Linux&#xA0;3.2.0-23-generic&#xA0;x86_64)</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;cd&#xA0;/srv</span></span></div></pre></div>

  <h1 class="package-name">
    <a href="/package/level-z">level-z</a>
      <i class="icon-public"></i>
  </h1>
  <p class="package-description">Z-order curve index for level-db</p>

  <form class="star">
    <input type="hidden" name="name" value="level-z">
    <input id="star-input" type="checkbox" name="isStarred" value="true" >
    <label for="star-input" class="icon-star"></label>
      <input type="hidden" name="crumb" value="D-ebB98_XbFeHADBP1YqGAKIH3sCr799JyqPeRvbd_7"/>
  </form>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 id="user-content-level-z" class="deep-link package-name-redundant"><a href="#level-z">level-z</a></h1>
<p>levelZ creates a sublevel db with the passed in name, that will insert items using
their z-order index, so they can easily be queried by location. Items can still
be retrieved efficiently by their primary id (this now requires 2 lookups rather than 1).</p>
<p>the new db has the following methods:</p>
<ul>
<li>get: get entry by original id</li>
<li>put: insert an item by id, item should also have lat/long keys (items currently do not support being moved)</li>
<li>del: delete an item</li>
<li>createReadStream: default level readstream (note that keys are a z-order index, rather than insert key)</li>
<li>inBoundingBox: inBoundingBox: returns a stream of entries within (or close to) the bounding box.
takes 1 arg: [[xMin, xMax], [yMin, yMax]]</li>
</ul>

    <a href="/package/z-index-manager">z-index-manager</a>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 id="user-content-z-index-manager" class="deep-link package-name-redundant"><a href="#z-index-manager">Z-Index Manager</a></h1>
<h2 id="user-content-what-is-z-index-manager" class="deep-link"><a href="#what-is-z-index-manager">What is Z-Index Manager?</a></h2>
<p class="package-description-redundant">Z-Index Manager will easily manage highest and lowest z-indexes on the DOM.</p>
<h2 id="user-content-how-to-use" class="deep-link"><a href="#how-to-use">How to Use</a></h2>
<p><strong>js</strong></p>

<div class="content-column">

  <h1 class="package-name">
    <a href="/package/z-builtins">z-builtins</a>
      <i class="icon-public"></i>
  </h1>
  <p class="package-description">JavaScript builtin mixins for Z</p>

  <form class="star">
    <input type="hidden" name="name" value="z-builtins">
    <input id="star-input" type="checkbox" name="isStarred" value="true" >
    <label for="star-input" class="icon-star"></label>
      <input type="hidden" name="crumb" value="KGhzsenGYuCcwUi0qAeOml1fWLUoKGQzAWVrv95jY3F"/>
  </form>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 class="package-name-redundant">z-builtins <a href="http://travis-ci.org/jakobmattsson/z-builtins"><img src="https://secure.travis-ci.org/jakobmattsson/z-builtins.png" class="badge"></a></h1>
<p>A plugin for <a href="https://github.com/jakobmattsson/z-core">Z</a>, the utility library for JavaScript promises.</p>
<p>The z-builtins plugin exposes all native JavaScript methods directly on Z promises.</p>
<h2 id="user-content-installation" class="deep-link"><a href="#installation">Installation</a></h2>
<p>The easiest way to get started is to use a ready-made package of Z, like <a href="https://github.com/jakobmattsson/z-core">z-std-pack</a>. It includes this plugin.</p>
<hr>
<p>If you want to set it up yourself, you have a number of options:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>npm install z-builtins</code> and then <code>var zBuiltins = require(&apos;z-builtins&apos;);</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>bower install z-builtins</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Download it manually from the dist folder of this repo.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>When installed, you apply the plugin by calling <code>Z.mixin(zBuiltins)</code>. Note that you have to install <a href="https://github.com/jakobmattsson/z-core">Z</a> first, if you&apos;re not using a ready-made package.</p>
<h2 id="user-content-crash-course" class="deep-link"><a href="#crash-course">Crash course</a></h2>
<p>Go to the <a href="https://github.com/jakobmattsson/z-core">Z main page</a> to learn what Z does.</p>
<p>The idea behind this particular plugin, <strong>z-builtins</strong>, is to expose all the standard JavaScript methods available on strings, arrays and other types of objects directly on promises wrapping them. It allows you to do things like:</p>

js"><span>)</span></span></span></span><span class="punctuation terminator statement js"><span>;</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>&#xA0;</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span class="comment line double-slash js"><span class="punctuation definition comment js"><span>//</span></span><span>&#xA0;Even&#xA0;global&#xA0;methods&#xA0;like&#xA0;&quot;console.log&quot;&#xA0;are</span><span>&#xA0;</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span class="comment line double-slash js"><span class="punctuation definition comment js"><span>//</span></span><span>&#xA0;available&#xA0;directly&#xA0;on&#xA0;our&#xA0;objects&#xA0;now.</span><span>&#xA0;</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span class="variable other object js"><span>listOfToddlers</span></span><span class="meta js"><span class="meta delimiter method period js"><span>.</span></span><span class="entity name function js"><span>log</span></span><span class="meta js"><span class="punctuation definition begin round js"><span>(</span></span><span class="punctuation definition end round js"><span>)</span></span></span></span><span class="punctuation terminator statement js"><span>;</span></span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>All the usual methods are available directly on promises. Instead of returning their results directly (which would be impossible, since the promise might not have resolved) they in turn return new promises. Those new promises also have all the expected methods. And so on. Down to turtles.</p>
<p>The only time you have to treat these objects diferently then you have treated regular objects is when you call global functions like <code>console.log</code>. If the list of toddlers from above was used like this, then <code>console.log(listOfToddlers)</code> would just print <code>&quot;[object Object]&quot;</code> since  <code>listOfToddlers</code> is not actually as string; it&apos;s a promise. Instead, either do <code>listOfToddlers.then(function(list) { console.log(list)); };</code> or simply <code>listOfToddlers.log()</code>.</p>
<h2 id="user-content-methods-included-in-this-plugin" class="deep-link"><a href="#methods-included-in-this-plugin">Methods included in this plugin</a></h2>
<p>Except then explicitly noted, all methods below will invoke their <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects">native counterparts</a> directly. All quirks and bugs will still get to you. As will all fixes and performance improvements in the future.</p>
<h3 id="user-content-string-methods" class="deep-link"><a href="#string-methods">String methods</a></h3>
<div class="highlight js"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>charAt</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>charCodeAt</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>concat</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>indexOf</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>lastIndexOf</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>localeCompare</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>replace</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>search</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>slice</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>split</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>substr</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>substring</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>toLocaleLowerCase</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>toLocaleUpperCase</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>toLowerCase</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>toString&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span><span class="constant other js"><span>AND</span></span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span><span>&#xA0;toStr</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>toUpperCase</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>trim</span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>Note that <code>toString</code> has not been overridden to return a promise. It will return a string as always. That is to follow the principle of least surprise. If you want to call <code>toString</code> on the value that the promise resolves to, then you can use <code>toStr</code>.</p>

js"><span>slice</span></span><span class="meta js"><span class="punctuation definition begin round js"><span>(</span></span><span class="constant numeric decimal js"><span>0</span></span><span <h3 id="user-content-array-methods" class="deep-link"><a href="#array-methods">Array methods</a></h3>
<div class="highlight js"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>pop&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>push&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>reverse&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>shift&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>sort&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>splice&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>unshift&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>concat</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>join</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>slice</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>toString&#xA0;</span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span><span class="constant other js"><span>AND</span></span><span class="keyword operator js"><span>*</span></span><span>&#xA0;toStr&#xA0;</span><span class="comment line double-slash js"><span class="punctuation definition comment js"><span>//</span></span><span>&#xA0;same&#xA0;as&#xA0;String.toString,&#xA0;earlier&#xA0;in&#xA0;the&#xA0;docs</span><span>&#xA0;</span></span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>toLocaleString</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>indexOf</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>lastIndexOf</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>forEach</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>every</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>some</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>filter</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>map</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>reduce</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>reduceRight</span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>The methods followed by a star are mutator methods in the JavaScript standard library. They change the object they act upon and return something else.</p>
<p>Mutating behaviour doesn&apos;t work well with promises. Therefore, these methods do <strong>not</strong> mutate when used in Z. Their usual return values are ignored and instead they return the new array produced.</p>

<h3 id="user-content-global-functions" class="deep-link"><a href="#global-functions">Global functions</a></h3>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>eval</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>isFinite</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>isNaN</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>parseFloat</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>parseInt</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>decodeURI</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>decodeURIComponent</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>encodeURI</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>encodeURIComponent</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>escape</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>unescape</span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>These functions use the promised value as their first argument. Remaining arguments can be given as usual.</p>

<h3 id="user-content-other-methods" class="deep-link"><a href="#other-methods">Other methods</a></h3>
<div class="highlight js"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>length</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>isArray</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>log</span></span></div><div class="line"><span class="source js"><span>print</span></span></div></pre></div>
<p>The <code>length</code> method returns the value of the length property.</p>
<p>The <code>isArray</code> method invokes <code>Array.iArray</code>.</p>
<p>The <code>log</code> method invoked <code>console.log</code>.</p>
<p>The <code>print</code> method invokes <code>JSON.stringify</code> followed by <code>console.log</code>.</p>

  <div id="readme" class="markdown">
      <h1 class="package-name-redundant">z-manager <a href="https://travis-ci.org/morishitter/z-manager"><img src="https://travis-ci.org/morishitter/z-manager.svg" class="badge"></a></h1>
<p class="package-description-redundant">Set z-index value relatively and manage easily.</p>
<h2 id="user-content-installation" class="deep-link"><a href="#installation">Installation</a></h2>
<div class="highlight"><pre class="editor editor-colors"><div class="line"><span class="text"><span>$&#xA0;npm&#xA0;install&#xA0;z-manager&#xA0;-g</span></span></div></pre></div>

<p>Sort property in ascending order of z-index value you want.</p>
<p>and, run bellow command:</p>
